***изменить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>измени́ть</a> (1733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">из-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">мѣнити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">měniti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*měniti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>измени́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmenítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменять.html>изменя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change, to alter, to modify, to edit</li>
<li>to vary</li>
<li><i>(with dative)</i> to betray, to become unfaithful, to cheat on</li>
<li>to break, to violate <i>(an oath, promise)</i></li>
<li>to fail <i>(memory)</i></li>
<li>to desert</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измена.html>изме́на</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izména</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменение.html>измене́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izmenénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измениться.html>измени́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izmenítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменяться.html>изменя́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izmenjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(intransitive)</i></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:менять.html>меня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">menjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:нить.html>ни́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c(7).      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:изменять.html>изменя́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:встречаться.html>Встреча́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устаревший.html>устаре́вший</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:схема.html>схе́ме</a> 4b: <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ударение.html>ударе́нием</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рмах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наст.html>наст</a>. вр. — <i><a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>изменю́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>измени́т</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>изменя́т</a></i>.
</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>из-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-мен-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>. <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменник.html>изме́нник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izménnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменник.html>изме́нника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменник.html>изме́нники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменник.html>изме́нников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изме́нница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>traitor, betrayer</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изменять.html>изменя́ть</a> (5902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>измени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izmenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменять.html>изменя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmenjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изменить.html>измени́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change, to alter, to modify, to edit</li>
<li>to vary</li>
<li><i>(with dative)</i> to betray, to become unfaithful</li>
<li>to break, to violate (an oath, promise)</li>
<li>to fail (memory)</li>
<li>to desert</li></ol>

***изменяться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изменяться.html>изменя́ться</a> (9092)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:измерять.html>измеря́ть</a> (14143)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерять.html>измеря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmerjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерить.html>изме́рить</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерять.html>изме́рять</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to measure <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">ascertain the quantity of a unit</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cheat in measuring, to give short measure</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>измеря́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmerjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">изме́риться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>изме́ряться</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to measure <i>(a stated size)</i>, to amount <i>(to)</i>, to be as large [long, deep, etc] <i>(as)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>измеряется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>тридцатью́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:метр.html>ме́трами</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dérevo izmerjajetsja tridcatʹjú métrami</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the tree measures 30 metres</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́сы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уголь.html>угля</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:измеряться.html>измеряются</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:миллион.html>миллио́нами</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тонна.html>то́нн</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zapásy uglja izmerjajutsja milliónami tonn</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the coal reserves amount to [are as large as] millions of tons</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:измерять.html>измеря́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izmerjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***изможденный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:изможденный.html>измождённый</a> (15384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">измъжденъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izmŭždenŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, past passive participle of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">измъждити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">izmŭžditi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мозжи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mozžítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to ache dully but persistently</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мо́зглый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mózglyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dank; frail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, dialectal <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мо́згнуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mózgnutʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spoil, to perish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мзга</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mzga</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wet weather</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изможденный.html>измождённый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">izmoždjónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>haggard, peaked</li></ol>
